regionList = [re.search('^([A-Z]+)', i.strip()).group(1) for i in tableList]
constituencyList = [re.search('Constituency:[\s+\!]*([A-Z]+)', i.strip()).group(1) for i in tableList]
totalVotesCast = [re.search('Total Votes Cast: (.*?)\s+', i).group(1) for i in a]
turnOutList = [re.search('Turn-Out: (.*%)$', i.strip()).group(1) for i in b]
dfResult = pd.DataFrame({'Region':regionList,
                         'Constutuency':constituencyList,
                        'TotalVotesCast':totalVotesCast,
                        'Turn-out':turnOutList})
dfResult.head()
